BitsStates ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS     deprecated
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Bit String providing a status summary for all
		alarms defined in this MIB module. A bit is set
		to one if the state of that alarm is 'fail'."
	SYNTAX  BITS {
		transmittedPowerMinor (0),
		transmittedPowerMajor (1),
		channelBERMinor (2),
		channelBERMajor (3),
		trtCurrentsOutRange (4),
		temperature (5),
		reflectedPower (6),
		unlockTS (7),
		noInputSignal (8),
		asiError (9),
		mipError (10),
		ppsError (11),
		iFDVBTSignal (12),
		gps10MHz (13),
		powerAmplifierCommunication (14),
		moduleCommunication (15),
		powerSupply1 (16),
		powerSupply2 (17),
		externalSupply (18),
		gpsHoldover (19),
		gpsAntenna (20)
	}


Mutes ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Mutes status.
		
		Bit - Mutes
		1 - MPEG Error (lsb)
		2 - No MIP
		3 - GPS
		4 - ASI
		5 - MPEG overflow
		6 - SFN error
		"
	SYNTAX  BITS {
		null0 (0),
		null1 (1),
		sfnError (2),
		mpegOverflow (3),
		asi (4),
		gps (5),
		noMIP (6),
		mpegError (7)
	}


RateStatus ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"RateStatus is used in trap control 
		                            
		                            1: disabled 2: enabled 3: enabledPeriod"
	SYNTAX  INTEGER {
		disabled (1),
		enabled (2),
		enabledPeriod (3)
	}

		noRedundance (1),

		5: Compact Serie"

		systemReadConfigurations (6),
		hardwareResetMuxs (7)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"If the manager writes in this variable:
		
		1 = it does not efect (telecontrol is ON and polling the modules)
		2 = telecontrol system will be reboot (telecontrol application)
		3 = telecontrol system will be soft reset (reboot with actual values)
		4 = telecontrol system will be hard reset (reboot with default values)
		5 = telecontrol system will find new modules connected to the control bus
		6 = telecontrol system will read module configurations - Obsolete in Compact Range
		7 = telecontrol system will resets MUXs
		"
	::= { adminDBTM 3 }

snmpTrapControlRateStatus  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     RateStatus
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This object is used for rate control of traps,
		preventing overload of the management network
		by transmission of an excessive number of traps.
		The value 'disabled' means that traps are never
		sent. The value 'enabled' means that a trap will
		be sent when triggered.
		                            
		When a trap is sent, the agent changes the value
		of this object to 'enabledPeriod'. In this
		state the agent will not send any more traps.
		The agent automatically changes the value back
		to 'enabled' when the time specified by
		alarmTrapControlPeriod
		expires. A management application may set the
		value to 'enabled' at any time, but must never
		set the value to 'enabledPeriod'.
		"
	::= { snmpTrapsConfiguration 2 }

snmpTrapControlPeriod  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32
	UNITS 	"seconds"
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"The agent will ensure that the interval between
		sending traps is no shorter than this time period
		(unless overridden by the manager)."
	::= { snmpTrapsConfiguration 3 }

snmpTrapsSync  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This value is the last sent trap number. It is used for synchronizing the traps.
		
		If the remote user writes this variable with a number lower than actual,
		the agent will send the traps since that number to the actual.
		"
	::= { snmpTrapsConfiguration 4 }

snmpTrapsAuthTrapEnable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     TruthValue
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Setting this variable to 1enables generation of authentication failure traps.
		
		True = authentication failure traps disable
		False  = authentication failure traps enable
		
		"
	::= { snmpTrapsConfiguration 5 }

snmpTrapsCommunity  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     OCTET STRING (SIZE(1..32))
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This define the default comunity string to be used when sending traps.
		
		1..32 characters"

	MAX-ACCESS read-write

	DESCRIPTION 
		"The agent will send one trap if passed 
		this amount of seconds has not been sent no alarm

snmpFastTrapsSync  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     TruthValue
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Fast Trap Syncronization sends to SNMP Managers

ucaTable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF UcaEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This table contains the basic information of each UCA connected to the system."
	::= { uca 1 }

ucaEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX 	UcaEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Each row is UCA information. There 1 UCA for each subrack."
	INDEX { ucaIndex }
	::= { ucaTable 1 }

UcaEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	ucaIndex
		Integer32,
	ucaCtrlAddress
		Integer32,
	ucaMux1OnOffReset
		INTEGER,
	ucaMux2OnOffReset
		INTEGER,
	ucaMux3OnOffReset
		INTEGER,
	ucaStatusAlarm
		BitsStates,
	ucaHysteresis
		Integer32,
	ucaFirmware
		DisplayString,
	ucaTrapsConfiguration
		BitsStates
}

ucaIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (1..6)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"UCA index"
	::= { ucaEntry 1 }

ucaCtrlAddress  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (20..25)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Control address."
	::= { ucaEntry 2 }

ucaMux1OnOffReset  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		ucaMux1On (1),
		ucaMux1Off (2),
		ucaMux1Reset (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"MUX 1 Status. 
		
		1 = On
		2 = Off
		3 = This MUX will be reset"
	::= { ucaEntry 3 }

ucaMux2OnOffReset  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		ucaMux2On (1),
		ucaMux2Off (2),
		ucaMux2Reset (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"MUX 2 Status.
		
		1 = On
		2 = Off
		3 = This MUX will be reset"
	::= { ucaEntry 4 }

ucaMux3OnOffReset  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		ucaMux3On (1),
		ucaMux3Off (2),
		ucaMux3Reset (3)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"MUX 3 Status. 
		
		1 = On
		2 = Off
		3 = This MUX will be reset"
	::= { ucaEntry 5 }

ucaStatusAlarm  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     BitsStates
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     deprecated
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Alarm bits status for this UCA"
	::= { ucaEntry 6 }

ucaHysteresis  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32
	UNITS 	"dsec"
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Time to validate the alarm status."
	::= { ucaEntry 7 }

ucaFirmware  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"UCA Firmware version"
	::= { ucaEntry 8 }

ucaTrapsConfiguration  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     BitsStates
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     deprecated
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Bits array for enable/disable the traps from this module
		
		For each bit:
		     False: disable
		     true: enable
		
		The bits are represented in BitsStates convection"
	::= { ucaEntry 9 }

gpsTable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF GpsEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This table contains the basic information of each GPS connected to the system."
	::= { gps 1 }

gpsEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX 	GpsEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Each row is GPS information."
	INDEX { gpsIndex }
	::= { gpsTable 1 }

GpsEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	gpsIndex
		Integer32,
	gpsCtrlAddress
		Integer32,
	gpsSatellites
		Integer32,
	gpsStatusAlarm
		BitsStates,
	gpsHysteresis
		Integer32,
	gpsFirmware
		DisplayString,
	gpsTrapsConfiguration
		BitsStates,
	gpsLatitude
		DisplayString,
	gpsLongitude
		DisplayString,
	gpsAltitude
		DisplayString,
	gpsState
		INTEGER,
	gpsGMTdate
		DisplayString,
	gpsHardware
		DisplayString,
	gpsHoldoverDrift
		Integer32
}

gpsIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (1..2)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"GPS index."
	::= { gpsEntry 1 }

gpsCtrlAddress  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (50..51)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Control address."
	::= { gpsEntry 2 }

gpsSatellites  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (0..8)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Number of locked satellites."
	::= { gpsEntry 3 }

	SYNTAX     BitsStates
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     deprecated
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Alarm bits status for this GPS"

	MAX-ACCESS read-only

	::= { gpsEntry 6 }

gpsTrapsConfiguration  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     BitsStates
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     deprecated
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Bits array for enable/disable the traps from this module
		
		For each bit:
		     False: disable
		     true: enable
		
		The bits are represented in BitsStates convection"
	::= { gpsEntry 7 }

gpsLatitude  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION

	::= { gpsEntry 8 }

		"Longitude of the GPS antenna"
	::= { gpsEntry 9 }

gpsAltitude  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Altitude of the GPS antenna"
	::= { gpsEntry 10 }

gpsState  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		gpsStarting (1),
		gpsUnlocked (2),
		gpsHoldover (3),
		gpsLocked (4)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"GPS state:
		
		1: starting (before GPS module communication)
		2: unlocked - it is not synchronized (error is higher thandrift configuration)
		3: holdover - Synchronization error is lower than drift configuration
		4: locked - boad is synchronized to the reference"
	::= { gpsEntry 11 }

gpsGMTdate  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Show GMT from GPS board (GMT when synchronized)"
	::= { gpsEntry 12 }

gpsHardware  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     DisplayString
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"GPS hardware information.
		
		Nowadays it could be:
		EBO2 - EBO 2th version 
		EBO3 - EBO 3th version"
	::= { gpsEntry 13 }

gpsHoldoverDrift  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (0..255)
	UNITS 	"usec"
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"GPS Drift in holdover mode in microsecond.
		
		"
	::= { gpsEntry 14 }

	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		splitterNullOutput (1),
		splitterGPS1Output (2),
		splitterGPS2Output (3),
		splitterExternalOutput (4)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Actived output
		
		1: Output Null
		2: GPS 1
		3: GPS 2
		4: External output"
	::= { gpsSplitterEntry 3 }

gpsSplitterCommunicationAlarm  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     TruthValue
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"GPS splitter Commnication 
		
		False: there is communication
		True: there is not communication, so module is alarmed"
	::= { gpsSplitterEntry 4 }

gpsSplitterGPS1Status  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		gpsDisconnected (1),
		gpsDetected (2),
		gpsConnected (3),
		gpsNotConfigured (4),
		gpsUnlocked (5),
		gpsLocked (6),
		gpsHoldover (7),
		gpsPostHoldover (8),
		gpsBrokenDown (9),
		gpsNotDetected (10),
		gpsSfnNok (11)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"GPS 1 status
		
		1: Disconnect
		2: Detected
		3: Connected
		4: Not configured
		5: Unlocked
		6: Locked
		7: Holdover
		8: Post-Holdover
		9: Broken down
		10: Not detected
		11: SFN nok
		"
	::= { gpsSplitterEntry 5 }

dvbs2AsiRedundanceTable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF Dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"An input (RF B) is redundant from another one (RF A) by cloning the configuration.
		The ouput configurated for RF A, will switch to RF B after hysteresis time."
	::= { dvbs2Asi 1 }

dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX 	Dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"There are 4 RF inputs, so 4 redundance possibilities"
	INDEX { reduncandeRfIndex, 
		redundanceRfModuleIndex }
	::= { dvbs2AsiRedundanceTable 1 }

Dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	redundanceRfModuleIndex
		Integer32,
	redundanceRfCtrlAddress
		Integer32,
	reduncandeRfIndex
		Integer32,
	redundanceInput
		INTEGER
}

redundanceRfModuleIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (1..255)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"For each dvb-s2 / ASI module, it will be a redundancy table"
	::= { dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry 1 }

redundanceRfCtrlAddress  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (-1|1..255)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Control Address for this module"
	::= { dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry 2 }

reduncandeRfIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (1..4)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"For each module, would be 4 RF inputs"
	::= { dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry 3 }

redundanceInput  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		rf1 (1),
		rf2 (2),
		rf3 (3),
		rf4 (4),
		auxRf1 (5),
		auxRf2 (6),
		auxRf3 (7),
		auxRf4 (8),
		notRedundance (9)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-write
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Configure a redundancy for this module
		
		Configure other input redundance from this - rf1, rf2, rf3, rf4
		This input is configurated like auxiliar from other - auxRf1, auxRf2, auxRf3, auxRf4"
	::= { dvbs2AsiRedundanceEntry 4 }

dvbs2AsiInputRfTable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF Dvbs2AsiInputRfEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Configure the ASI inputs"
	::= { dvbs2Asi 2 }

dvbtAlarmTrapTable  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX SEQUENCE OF DvbtAlarmTrapEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This table holds the last 100 traps sent to managing stations."
	::= { dvbtBroadcastAlarm 30 }

dvbtAlarmTrapEntry  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX 	DvbtAlarmTrapEntry
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"An entry in the alarmTrapTable."
	INDEX { alarmTrapIndex }
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapTable 1 }

DvbtAlarmTrapEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	alarmTrapIndex
		Integer32,
	eventIdTrap
		Integer32,
	notificationIdTrap
		Integer32,
	perceivedSeverityTrap
		INTEGER,
	timeStampTrap
		OCTET STRING,
	additionalTextTrap
		OCTET STRING
}

alarmTrapIndex  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (1..100)
	MAX-ACCESS not-accessible
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"Index in the alarmTrapTable."
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapEntry 1 }

eventIdTrap  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32 (1..6)
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This is an integer uniquely identifying the notification and an indication 
		of the order in which the notifications were generated by the agent.
		
		Note that the agent does not guarantee that its sequencing reflects 
		the order of the underlying events from which the notifications were generated."
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapEntry 2 }

notificationIdTrap  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     Integer32
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This is a number identifying the trap (enventID) which has being ceased."
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapEntry 3 }

perceivedSeverityTrap  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     INTEGER {
		critical (1),
		major (2),
		minor (3),
		warning (4),
		cleared (5)
	}
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This attribute describes the severity of the cause of the trap.
		The attribute can take the following values:
		
		Critical (1)
		Major (2)
		Minor (3)
		Warning (4)
		Cleared (5)
		"
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapEntry 4 }

timeStampTrap  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     OCTET STRING (SIZE(19))
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This is a timestamp indicating the time at which the notification was generated
		
		hh:mm:ss dd/MM/YYYY"
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapEntry 5 }

additionalTextTrap  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX     OCTET STRING (SIZE(0..48))
	MAX-ACCESS read-only
	STATUS     current
	DESCRIPTION 
		"This attribute is a string that provides the RF reference 
		(or phisical y this module is not a RF module) reference.
		
		Typical values:
		
		'Gap Filler RF 68 [Ctrl 2]'  i's mean that this trap 
		
		'UCA subrack 2 [Ctrl 22] it's meaning "
	::= { dvbtAlarmTrapEntry 6 }

fanAlarm1Trap  NOTIFICATION-TYPE

		notificationIdTrap, 
		perceivedSeverityTrap, 
		timeStampTrap, 
		additionalTextTrap }
